commons insecure

functions like strcpy,

gets etc. Use the

compiler option -

D_FORTIFY_SOURCE=2

to fortify functions.

This check is not

applicable for

Dart/Flutter libraries.

has NX bit

set. This

marks a

memory

page non-

executable

making

attacker

injected

shellcode

non-

Dynamic

Shared

Object (DSO)

info

The shared

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

overwrite

GOT

entries.

RELRO.

STRIPPED STRIPPED 52 armeabi-v7a/libnative-filters.so

True

info

The binary

has NX bit

set. This

marks a

memory

page non-

executable

making

attacker

injected

shellcode

non-

executable.

Dynamic

Shared

Object (DSO)

info

The shared

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

None

info

The

binary

does not

have run-

time

search

path or

RPATH

set.

None

info

The binary

does not have

RUNPATH set.

False

warning

The binary does not

have any fortified

functions. Fortified

functions provides

buffer overflow checks

against glibc's

commons insecure

functions like strcpy,

gets etc. Use the

compiler option -

D_FORTIFY_SOURCE=2

to fortify functions.

This check is not

applicable for

Dart/Flutter libraries.

info

Symbols are

stripped.

True

info

The binary

has NX bit

set. This

marks a

memory

page non-

executable

making

attacker

injected

shellcode

non-

executable.

Dynamic

Shared

Object (DSO)

info

The shared

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

None

info

The

binary

does not

have run-

time

search

path or

RPATH

set.

None

info

The binary

does not have

RUNPATH set.

False

warning

The binary does not

have any fortified

functions. Fortified

functions provides

buffer overflow checks

against glibc's

commons insecure

functions like strcpy,

gets etc. Use the

compiler option -

D_FORTIFY_SOURCE=2

to fortify functions.

This check is not

applicable for

Dart/Flutter libraries.

info

high

This shared

object does

not have

RELRO

enabled.

The entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) are

writable.

Without

this

compiler

flag, buffer

overflows

on a global

variable

can

overwrite

GOT

entries.

Use the

option -

z,relro,-

z,now to

enable full

RELRO and

only -

z,relro to

enable

partial

RELRO.

making

attacker

injected

shellcode

non-

executable.

Dynamic

Shared

Object (DSO)

info

The shared

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

None

info

The

binary

does not

have run-

time

search

path or

RPATH

set.

None

info

The binary

does not have

RUNPATH set.

info

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

None

info

The

binary

does not

have run-

time

search

path or

RPATH

set.

info

does not have

RUNPATH set.

RELRO

enabled.

The entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) are

writable.

Without

this

compiler

flag, buffer

overflows

on a global

variable

can

overwrite

GOT

entries.

Use the

option -

z,relro,-

z,now to

enable full

RELRO and

only -

z,relro to

enable

partial

RELRO.

independent

to the stack

the return

address.

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

object is

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

reliably.

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

Shared

Object (DSO)

info

The shared

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

False

high

This binary

does not

have a stack

canary

value added

to the stack.

Stack

canaries are

used to

detect and

prevent

exploits

from

overwriting

return

address.

Use the

option -

fstack-

protector-

all to

enable

stack

canaries.

Not

applicable

for

Dart/Flutter

libraries

unless Dart

FFI is used.

No RELRO

high

This shared

object does

not have

RELRO

enabled.

The entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) are

writable.

Without

this

compiler

flag, buffer

overflows

on a global

variable

can

overwrite

GOT

entries.

Use the

option -

z,relro,-

z,now to

enable full

RELRO and

only -

z,relro to

enable

partial

RELRO.

None

info

The

binary

does not

have run-

time

search

path or

RPATH

set.

None

info

The binary

does not have

RUNPATH set.

False

warning

The binary does not

have any fortified

functions. Fortified

functions provides

buffer overflow checks

against glibc's

commons insecure

functions like strcpy,

gets etc. Use the

compiler option -

D_FORTIFY_SOURCE=2

to fortify functions.

This check is not

applicable for

Dart/Flutter libraries.

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

difficult to

reliably.

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

info

object has

enabled.

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

Dynamic

Shared

Object (DSO)

info

The shared

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

No RELRO

high

This shared

object does

not have

RELRO

enabled.

The entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) are

writable.

Without

this

compiler

flag, buffer

overflows

on a global

variable

can

overwrite

GOT

entries.

Use the

option -

z,relro,-

z,now to

enable full

RELRO and

only -

z,relro to

enable

partial

RELRO.

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

None

info

The

binary

does not

have run-

time

search

path or

RPATH

set.

info

does not have

RUNPATH set.

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

info

The

binary

does not

have run-

time

search

path or

RPATH

set.

info

does not have

RUNPATH set.

object does

not have

RELRO

enabled.

The entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) are

writable.

Without

this

compiler

flag, buffer

overflows

on a global

variable

can

overwrite

GOT

entries.

Use the

option -

z,relro,-

z,now to

enable full

RELRO and

only -

z,relro to

enable

partial

RELRO.

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

Shared

Object (DSO)

info

The shared

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

True

info

The binary

has NX bit

set. This

marks a

memory

page non-

executable

making

attacker

injected

shellcode

non-

executable.

Dynamic

Shared

Object (DSO)

info

The shared

object is

build with -

fPIC flag

which

enables

Position

independent

code. This

makes Return

Oriented

Programming

(ROP) attacks

much more

difficult to

execute

reliably.

True

info

This binary

has a stack

canary

value added

to the stack

so that it

will be

overwritten

by a stack

buffer that

overflows

the return

address.

This allows

detection of

overflows

by verifying

the integrity

of the

canary

before

function

return.

Full RELRO

info

This shared

object has

full RELRO

enabled.

RELRO

ensures

that the

GOT

cannot be

overwritten

in

vulnerable

ELF

binaries. In

Full RELRO,

the entire

GOT (.got

and .got.plt

both) is

marked as

read-only.

None

info

The

binary

does not

have run-

time

search

path or

RPATH

set.

None

info

The binary

does not have

RUNPATH set.

False

warning

The binary does not

have any fortified

functions. Fortified

functions provides

buffer overflow checks

against glibc's

commons insecure

functions like strcpy,

gets etc. Use the

compiler option -

D_FORTIFY_SOURCE=2

to fortify functions.

This check is not

applicable for

Dart/Flutter libraries.
